If you want to check out this Venus Optics Lens on their <a href=\"https://www.venuslens.net/product/laowa-argus-33mm-f-0-95-cf-apo/\">Website Click Here &gt;&gt;</a></p> \n<p>I have been a fan of Venus Optics since I saw their lens line for the first time at the PhotoPlus Expo many years ago. At that time they were offering very high quality built fully manual lenses and I was very impressed! Since then I have not had the chance to review any of the lenses due to limited time and reviewing just the Sony stuff has kept me very busy. Recently however I have been reviewing more manual lenses like the 7Artisans line for example, and Venus reached out to me so I accepted the offer for a loaner. </p> \n<p>With all that being said, WOW this lens is impressive!!
